### [1] [Factorization of elastic, single, and double diffractive $pp$ scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07788)
*Philipp B. Aretz,Kyle Lee,Stella T. Schindler,Iain W. Stewart*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用有效场论技术，在Regge极限下对质子-质子（pp）弹性、单衍射和双衍射前向散射过程进行因子化，并指出用于电子-质子（ep）衍射的衍射部分子分布函数（PDFs）在pp衍射中不具备普适性；进一步证明了rapidity反常维度在ep与pp衍射间具有普适性，并可在振幅层面确定色单态（Pomeron）演化方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释为何ep衍射中使用的衍射PDFs不能作为pp衍射中的普适强子函数，并厘清不同过程中因子化结构的差异。

Method: 采用有效场论方法，在Regge极限（|t| ≪ s）下对pp前向衍射过程进行因子化分析，比较ep与pp衍射中hadronic functions的行为，并研究rapidity反常维度与Pomeron演化。

Result: 发现当|t| ∼ Λ_QCD²时，ep与pp衍射中的强子函数不同，故衍射PDFs不具普适性；但rapidity反常维度是普适的，且色单态演化方程可在振幅层面确定。

Conclusion: 衍射PDFs在ep与pp过程中不具普适性，但rapidity反常维度具有跨过程普适性，支持在振幅层面构建统一的Pomeron演化框架。

Abstract: We use effective field theory techniques to factorize elastic, single, and double diffractive forward $pp$ scattering in the Regge limit $|t|\ll s$, where $t$ is the squared momentum transfer. These processes involve a large rapidity gap and comprise about half the total $pp$ cross section. We explain why the diffractive PDFs appearing in $ep$ diffraction do not appear as universal hadronic functions for $pp$ diffraction. For $|t|\sim Λ_{\rm QCD}^2$, we show that the hadronic functions in $ep$ and $pp$ diffraction differ, and hence are non-universal. In general, we prove that rapidity anomalous dimensions are universal between diffractive $ep$ and $pp$ processes, and that color-singlet (Pomeron) evolution equations can be determined at the amplitude level.

</details>


### [2] [PDF effects in high-mass Drell-Yan SMEFT analyses across flavour space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07791)
*David Marzocca,Manuel Morales-Alvarado*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了在高能SMEFT拟合中，部分子分布函数（PDF）不确定性对不同夸克味结构有效算符约束的影响，发现PDF拟合对第一代夸克相关算符的灵敏度削弱最显著，而角分布信息有助于缓解SMEFT与PDF之间的简并。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高质Drell-Yan双轻子过程是探测SMEFT中半轻子四费米子算符的敏感探针，但其对大-x区域PDF不确定性的依赖可能掩盖或模拟新物理信号，需厘清PDF拟合对不同味结构SMEFT算符约束的影响程度。

Method: 通过联合拟合SMEFT威尔逊系数与PDF伴生参数，系统分析PDF拟合对不同夸克味结构有效算符约束的影响，并评估角分布信息对缓解SMEFT-PDF简并的作用。

Result: PDF拟合导致SMEFT灵敏度呈强味依赖性退化：第一代夸克相关算符受最大影响，因其与主导高质谱的高-x价夸克光度强关联；重夸克算符受影响较小但存在算符依赖差异；角信息可有效降低SMEFT方向间及SMEFT-PDF间的简并。

Conclusion: PDF不确定性在高能SMEFT拟合中的重要性并非在味空间中均匀分布，必须进行味依赖性评估；角分布是提升SMEFT解析能力的关键工具。

Abstract: High-mass Drell-Yan dilepton production provides one of the most sensitive probes of semileptonic four-fermion operators in the Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT), thanks to the energy growth of the corresponding contributions. At the same time, these measurements also constrain parton distribution functions (PDFs) in the large-$x$ region, where PDF uncertainties can mimic or obscure smooth new-physics effects. In this work we study how the impact of PDF profiling on SMEFT constraints depends on the quark-flavour structure of the effective operators, by performing a joint fit of SMEFT Wilson coefficients and PDF nuisance parameters. We find that PDF profiling induces a strongly flavour-dependent degradation of the SMEFT sensitivity, both with current data and in HL-LHC projections. The largest broadenings occur for operators involving first-generation quarks, whose effects are correlated with the high-$x$ valence-quark luminosities that dominate the high-mass spectrum. Operators involving heavier quark flavours are less affected, although with non-negligible operator-dependent variations. As a byproduct of our analysis, we obtain an estimate on the changes induced in the PDF sector by profiling SMEFT effects. We also show that angular information provides an important handle to reduce degeneracies among SMEFT directions and between SMEFT effects and allowed PDF deformations. These results demonstrate that the relevance of PDF uncertainties in high-energy SMEFT fits is not uniform across flavour space, and must be assessed in a flavour-dependent way.

</details>


### [3] [Dissecting Parton Showers with Multi-Point Energy Correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07792)
*Mark Gonzalez,Philip Harris,Kyle Lee,Ian Moult,Simon Rothman*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了喷注子结构中四点能量关联器的唯象学，通过分析其在不同因子化通道上的投影，结合Herwig和Pythia模拟与解析计算，区分了本征自旋关联与运动学方位角关联，并指出在实验可及区域自旋关联较弱，呼吁进行完整的QCD四点关联器计算以检验部分子喷注模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 能量关联器具有高度微分特性，是探测喷注内多共线因子化和方位角结构的理想探针；四点关联器尚未被实验测量，其唯象学研究有助于检验新一代部分子喷注模型。

Method: 识别实验上可实现的四点关联器投影以探测不同因子化通道；使用Herwig和Pythia进行详细唯象模拟；对比部分子喷注结果与运动学极限下的解析计算，分离自旋与运动学方位角关联；提出实验可用的参数化形式与分析算法。

Result: 在实验可及运动学区域内，本征自旋关联显著弱于运动学方位角关联；验证了四点关联器对因子化通道的敏感性；提供了可用于LHC实验测量的具体参数化和分析方法。

Conclusion: 四点能量关联器有望成为LHC上检验下一代部分子喷注模型的关键观测量，但需完整QCD计算以支持实验解读与理论比对。

Abstract: The last several years have seen tremendous progress in the ability to both compute and measure multi-point correlations in energy flux. The highly differential nature of energy correlators makes them ideal probes of multi-collinear factorization and azimuthal structure within jets. In this paper, we explore the phenomenology of four-point correlators in jet substructure. We identify experimentally realizable projections that probe different factorization channels onto splitting tensors and splitting functions. We perform a detailed phenomenological study using both Herwig and Pythia. By comparing parton shower results with analytic calculations in kinematic limits, we are able to disentangle intrinsic spin correlations from kinematic azimuthal correlations. In experimentally accessible kinematic regions, we find the spin correlations are subdominant, strongly motivating a complete calculation of the four-point correlator in QCD to provide a test of the parton shower results. We also present parameterizations and analysis algorithms that can be used experimentally. Our work sets the stage for the experimental measurement of these observables at the LHC, and their use as probes of the next generation of parton showers.

</details>


### [4] [Flavor Hierarchies the Right Way](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07794)
*Pavel Fileviez Perez,Clara Murgui*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于普适跷跷板机制的费米子质量生成框架，通过引入阿贝尔规范对称性、矢量型费米子和标量场扩展标准模型，解释了带电费米子质量等级、中微子小质量及CP破坏相位（CKM相位），同时自然解决强CP问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决标准模型中费米子质量等级结构、中微子质量起源、CP破坏来源以及强CP问题等未解难题，寻求一个统一且自然的扩展框架。

Method: 构建包含新阿贝尔规范对称性、矢量型费米子和标量场的扩展模型；利用普适跷跷板机制生成带电费米子质量；通过中性扇区马约拉纳跷跷板产生轻中微子质量；借助Nelson-Barr结构在树图水平使QCD真空角为零；CP对称性在紫外区精确，在红外区由标量场真空期望值自发破缺。

Result: 成功统一解释费米子质量等级、中微子质量、CKM相位，并自然抑制强CP问题；矢量型费米子可处于TeV能标；新阿贝尔对称性破缺能标可较低，满足电偶极矩（EDM）实验限制。

Conclusion: 该框架为多个基本问题提供了简洁、自洽且可检验的统一解释，是标准模型有希望的扩展方向。

Abstract: We propose a framework for fermion mass generation based on a universal seesaw. The Standard Model is extended by an Abelian gauge symmetry acting on right-handed fermions, together with vector-like fermions and scalar fields. The ordinary Yukawa couplings are forbidden, except for the top-quark coupling to the Higgs, which is allowed at the renormalizable level and remains unsuppressed. The charged-fermion hierarchies then arise from mixing with the vector-like sector, and light neutrino masses emerge from a neutral sector Majorana seesaw. CP is exact in the ultraviolet and broken spontaneously by scalar vacuum expectation values. The resulting CP-violating phase is transmitted to the quark sector and generates the CKM phase, while a Nelson-Barr structure, realized through the universal seesaw block form, keeps the physical QCD vacuum angle zero at tree level. Consistency with EDM bounds beyond tree level requires moderately suppressed Yukawa couplings between SM doublets to the vector-like sector. If the leading higher-dimensional operators are unsuppressed, the same requirement can favor a low breaking scale for the new Abelian symmetry. In this regime the vector-like fermions can lie at the TeV scale, with suppressed mixing with the electroweak sector. This framework provides a simple setting in which the hierarchies of charged-fermion masses, neutrino masses, and CP-violating parameters can be accounted for within a common extension of the Standard Model.

</details>


### [5] [Azimuthal momentum isotropization in the Quark-Gluon Plasma thermalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07796)
*Sergio Barrera Cabodevila,Xiaojian Du,Carlos A. Salgado,Bin Wu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究重离子碰撞初始态方位角各向异性在BEDA框架下的弛豫行为，发现各谐波系数存在清晰的弛豫时间层级，并指出p_T依赖的谐波系数随时间演化呈现向高动量偏移的现象，与实验数据一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上认为重离子碰撞初始方位角各向异性会因末态相互作用迅速消失，但在小系统碰撞中观测到的方位角关联可能依赖于这些初始各向异性，因此需重新评估其作用。

Method: 采用Boltzmann方程扩散近似（BEDA）框架，研究初始方位角各向异性（按谐波展开）的弛豫动力学，并分析p_T依赖的各谐波系数随时间的演化。

Result: 发现不同阶谐波系数具有明显不同的弛豫时间尺度（层级结构）；p_T依赖的谐波系数峰值随时间向更高横动量移动，该现象在唯象模拟中与实验观测相符。

Conclusion: 初始方位角各向异性在热化早期阶段并非完全被抹除，其非平凡的弛豫动力学可能对小系统碰撞中的方位角关联提供重要解释，BEDA框架能定性再现关键实验特征。

Abstract: Azimuthal anisotropies coming from the initial state of a heavy-ion collision have been historically disregarded in the study of thermalization because they are expected to be rapidly washed out due to final-state interactions. However, they may be important when one attempts to describe azimuthal correlations observed in the collisions of small systems. In this work, we study how these initial anisotropies relax in the context of the Boltzmann Equation in Diffusion Approximation (BEDA). We find a clear hierarchy in the relaxation time of the anisotropies in terms of each harmonic coefficient. We also explore the evolution of the $p_T$-dependent harmonic coefficients in time, finding a shift in the initial peak towards higher momenta that mimics the experimental data when we perform a phenomenologically motivated simulation.

</details>


### [6] [Impact of QED Radiation on SMEFT Constraints in Deep Inelastic Scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07811)
*Sonny Mantry,Jian-Wei Qiu,Jia-Yue Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了碰撞诱导的QED辐射对标准模型有效场论(SMEFT)约束的影响，发现虽然截面受到量级为一的修正，但纵向电子自旋不对称性仅受百分之几的影响，因此更适合作为SMEFT研究的可观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用深度非弹性散射(DIS)精确测量超出标准模型的新物理，需要在标准模型有效场论(SMEFT)框架下进行解释，而QED辐射可能影响这些测量的精度。

Method: 基于轻子分布和碎裂函数的联合QCD+QED因子化框架，研究碰撞诱导的QED辐射对DIS截面及纵向电子自旋不对称性的影响。

Result: QED辐射会显著改变DIS截面，并在某些运动学区域显著改变因子化相关的有效动量转移；截面受到量级为一的修正，而纵向电子自旋不对称性仅受百分之几的影响。

Conclusion: 纵向电子自旋不对称性比截面更稳健，是未来DIS实验中提取SMEFT约束的更优可观测量；研究为SoLID和电子-离子对撞机(EIC)提供了基准预测。

Abstract: Deep-inelastic scattering (DIS) provides a powerful probe of physics beyond the Standard Model through precision measurements interpreted within the Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT). We study the impact of collision-induced QED radiation on SMEFT constraints using the joint QCD+QED factorization framework based on lepton distribution and fragmentation functions. QED radiation can substantially modify DIS cross sections and, in some kinematic regions, significantly alter the effective momentum transfer relevant for factorization. We find that while cross sections receive order-one corrections, longitudinal electron spin asymmetries are affected only at the few-percent level, making them significantly more robust observables for SMEFT studies. Benchmark projections for SoLID and the Electron-Ion Collider are provided to demonstrate the impact of QED radiation for future precision DIS analyses and the extraction of SMEFT constraints.

</details>


### [7] [Neutrino Masses and Dark Matter Stability in 3HDMs with Minimal Non-Abelian Discrete Symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07853)
*Cesar Bonilla,Andres Layana-Ramirez*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了基于全局非阿贝尔离散对称性的极小三希格斯二重态模型（3HDM），同时解释中微子质量和暗物质稳定性；通过新对称性的自发破缺产生的残余Z2宇称稳定暗物质候选者，该候选者与树级I型跷跷板机制共同在一环图中生成中微子质量；S3和D4被确定为实现该框架的最小非阿贝尔群，并构建了符合当前中微子振荡数据的极小模型；模型在Yukawa和标量扇区均保持CP守恒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 同时解释中微子质量起源和暗物质稳定性这一双重问题，并寻求最简化的理论框架。

Method: 构建基于S3和D4等最小非阿贝尔离散对称性的三希格斯二重态模型，利用对称性自发破缺产生的残余Z2宇称稳定暗物质，并结合一环图机制与树级I型跷跷板机制生成中微子质量。

Result: 成功构造出满足当前中微子振荡实验数据、且在Yukawa和标量扇区均CP守恒的极小S3和D4 3HDM模型。

Conclusion: 非阿贝尔离散对称性可自然统一解释中微子质量与暗物质稳定性，S3和D4是最小可行对称性，对应模型具有可检验的唯象学特征。

Abstract: We present minimal three-Higgs-doublet models (3HDMs) based on global non-Abelian discrete symmetries that simultaneously explain neutrino masses and dark matter stability. A residual $Z_2$ parity from the spontaneous breaking of the new symmetry stabilizes the dark matter candidate, which runs in the loop generating neutrino masses at one loop alongside a tree-level type-I seesaw contribution. We identify $S_3$ and $D_4$ as the smallest non-Abelian groups realizing this framework and determine the minimal models in both cases that are consistent with current neutrino oscillation data. The resulting models conserve CP in both the Yukawa and scalar sectors.

</details>


### [8] [Lepton mixing from the $Δ(96)$ Modular Littlest Seesaw](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07865)
*Hai-Zhi Hao,Li-Na Yan,Xiang-Gan Liu,Cai-Chang Li*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次全面且模型无关地研究了基于有限模群Δ(96)的模化最小 seesaw 模型，构建了所有不可约表示下的向量值模形式（VVMFs），分类了对称性保持的不动点，并导出了低权和次低权三重VVMFs的对齐方式；通过穷尽扫描残余对称性，识别出35种现象学可行且互不等价的对称性破缺模式，给出超出传统CSD(n)结构的新PMNS矩阵列及新混合参数关联，模型高度可预测，可被JUNO、DUNE和T2HK等实验严格检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建基于Δ(96)模群的模块化最小seesaw模型，以实现对中微子质量与混合的统一、预测性解释，并超越现有CSD(n)与TM₁范式。

Method: 构造Δ(96)所有不可约表示下的向量值模形式（VVMFs），分类对称性保持的不动点，推导低权与次低权三重VVMFs的对齐，穷尽扫描带残余对称性的轻子 sectors（带电轻子、大气/太阳中微子），并分析其PMNS矩阵结构与参数预测。

Result: 识别出35种现象学可行且互不等价的对称性破缺模式（21种正常序、14种倒序）；得到超越CSD(n)结构的狄拉克中微子质量矩阵；预言新的PMNS矩阵列与混合角、CP相位间的新关联；给出中微子质量、混合角和CP相的窄范围预测。

Conclusion: Δ(96)模化最小seesaw框架具有强预测能力与丰富现象学，为中微子质量起源与味结构提供了新且可检验的理论路径。

Abstract: We perform the first comprehensive and model independent study of Modular Littlest Seesaw models based on the finite modular group $Δ(96)$. We construct the vector-valued modular forms (VVMFs) for all irreducible representations of modular $Δ(96)$, classify the inequivalent symmetry-preserving fixed points, and derive the corresponding alignments of the low-weight and next-to-lowest-weight triplet VVMFs. These results allow an exhaustive scan over the residual symmetries in the charged lepton, atmospheric neutrino, and solar neutrino sectors. We identify 35 phenomenologically viable and inequivalent breaking patterns, including 21 with normal ordering and 14 with inverted ordering. The resulting Dirac neutrino mass matrices go beyond the conventional CSD$(n)$ structure, yielding new fixed PMNS columns and novel correlations among the lepton mixing parameters beyond the TM$_1$ paradigm. The viable models are highly predictive, giving narrow ranges for neutrino masses, mixing parameters and CP phases, and can be stringently tested by upcoming experiments such as JUNO, DUNE and T2HK.

</details>


### [9] [QCD for electroweak precision measurements: Foundations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07908)
*George Sterman*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文回顾了强相互作用与电弱相互作用耦合的历史发展，强调QED、深度非弹性散射、轻子湮灭及强子对撞中的夸克-反夸克湮灭等关键过程如何推动QCD和标准模型的建立，并支撑高能精密电弱测量与新物理探索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用强相互作用与电弱相互作用之间的耦合关系，通过交叉验证和历史演进视角，深化对标准模型的理解并拓展新物理探索路径。

Method: 采用历史综述方法，梳理从QED到QCD再到标准模型建立的关键实验与理论进展，分析不同散射与湮灭过程在其中的作用。

Result: 系统阐明了深度非弹性散射、轻子湮灭和强子对撞中夸克-反夸克湮灭等过程如何促成QCD确立与标准模型完善，并指出这些方法持续支撑高能电弱精密测量与新物理搜寻。

Conclusion: 强与电弱相互作用的耦合不仅加深了我们对标准模型的认识，也为未来高精度检验和超越标准模型的新物理研究提供了坚实基础与方法论指导。

Abstract: The couplings of the strong to electroweak sectors of the Standard Model enable the exploration of each using our growing knowledge of the other. In this review, we will follow the sweep of history. Starting with QED as a precision theory, deep inelastic scattering served as a gateway to the strong interactions, followed by leptonic annihilation and quark-antiquark annihilation in hadron-hadron scattering. In turn, the resulting understanding of QCD helped establish the Standard Model. The same techniques form the basis for many precision electroweak measurements at high energy and searches for signs of new physics.

</details>


### [10] [Serendipitous supersymmetric solution to the strong CP problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07921)
*Howard Baer,Vernon Barger,Dibyashree Sengupta*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合MSSM、离散Z_n^R对称性与Kim-Nilles机制的框架，通过禁止μ项并利用PQ对称性破缺生成弱尺度μ项，同时自然引入DFSZ轴子以解决强CP问题，并提供SUSY DFSZ轴子作为暗物质候选者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决MSSM中μ项调谐、R-宇称破坏导致质子快速衰变以及维度-5质子衰变算符等问题，同时统一处理强CP问题和暗物质候选者。

Method: 引入与大统一相容的无反常离散Z_n^R对称性；利用Higgs场与PQ荷携带单态场X、Y耦合（Kim-Nilles机制）；在超对称破缺下再生μ项并同时破缺Z_n^R与U(1)_{PQ}全局对称性。

Result: 成功在MSSM中自然实现μ项生成、抑制质子衰变、解决强CP问题，并导出DFSZ轴子作为暗物质候选者；可能额外存在WIMP型暗物质，取决于诱导出的R-宇称破坏算符阶数。

Conclusion: 该框架将多个关键问题（μ问题、质子稳定性、强CP问题、暗物质）纳入统一对称性结构，表明SUSY模型可兼具理论自洽性与现象学丰富性。

Abstract: The Minimal Supersymmetric Standard Model (MSSM) has several problems: 1. its mu term must be forbidden, then regenerated at the weak scale, 2. it allows for R-parity violating superpotential terms which lead to rapid proton decay, 3. it allows for dimension-5 proton decay operators. The usual imposition of R- or matter parity P_M solves only the second of these, whereas anomaly-free discrete Z_n^R symmetries (consistent with grand unification) address all of them. Once the mu-term is forbidden, the MSSM develops an accidental global U(1)_{PQ} symmetry. By coupling the Higgs fields to PQ-charged gauge singlet fields X, Y (in the Kim-Nilles mechanism), and imposing SUSY breaking, one regenerates mu at the weak scale whilst breaking the discrete Z_n^R and the U(1)_{PQ}. The broken global U(1)_{PQ} develops a pseudo-Goldstone boson, the DFSZ axion, thus (perhaps inadvertently) solving the strong CP problem. In this setting, SUSY develops a dark matter candidate, the SUSY DFSZ axion, and possibly, though not necessarily, a WIMP dark matter candidate as well, depending on the order of the induced R-parity violating operators.

</details>


### [11] [Multipolar Dark Matter Freeze-out in an Early Matter-Dominated Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07956)
*Debajit Bose,Prolay Chanda,Suvam Maharana,Poulami Mondal*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 计算费米子暗物质通过磁偶极、电偶极、环偶极和电荷半径等高维电磁算符与标准模型相互作用时，在早期物质主导并伴随长寿命重场衰变引起熵注入的宇宙学背景下的冻结过程。

Result: 熵稀释大幅降低实现观测丰度所需的耦合强度，使部分在标准辐射主导宇宙中被直接探测和太阳中微子观测排除的参数空间重新变得可行。

Conclusion: 大爆炸核合成前的宇宙学历史显著影响电磁多极暗物质的现象学特征与实验可行性，需在暗物质模型构建与约束分析中予以考虑。

Abstract: The relic abundance of thermal dark matter depends not only on its particle interactions but also on the expansion history of the early Universe. We study the freeze-out of fermionic dark matter interacting with the Standard Model through higher-dimensional electromagnetic operators in an early matter-dominated cosmology. In particular, we consider magnetic dipole, electric dipole, anapole, and charge-radius interactions, and compute the couplings required to reproduce the observed dark matter relic abundance in the presence of entropy injection from the decay of a long-lived heavy field. The resulting parameter space is compared with that obtained in the standard radiation-dominated freeze-out scenario and confront it with current constraints from direct-detection experiments and solar neutrino observations. We find that the entropy dilution associated with an early matter-dominated epoch significantly reduces the interaction strength required to obtain the observed relic abundance, thereby rendering viable regions of parameter space that are excluded in the conventional cosmological history. Our results demonstrate that the cosmological history prior to Big Bang nucleosynthesis can have an important impact on the phenomenology and experimental viability of electromagnetic multipole dark matter.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质子质量主要并非来自希格斯机制，而是源于QCD真空的量子结构，特别是胶子迹反常；但该贡献缺乏直接实验探测途径。

Method: 利用标量引力形状因子作为探针，将胶子迹反常贡献与三个可观测量关联：深虚康普顿散射中的夸克标量引力形状因子、近阈值重夸克偶素产生中的胶子标量引力形状因子、以及核子sigma项形状因子。

Result: 成功构建出可实验提取的标量胶子迹形状因子，并发现其在强子尺度上与格点QCD计算和瞬子液体模型定量一致。

Abstract: Most of the proton mass originates not from the Higgs mechanism but from the quantum structure of the QCD vacuum. The dominant contribution arises from the gluonic trace anomaly associated with the breaking of conformal symmetry in quantum chromodynamics. We show that this anomaly contribution is experimentally accessible through scalar gravitational form factors. The key observable is the scalar gluonic trace form factor of the proton, which can be reconstructed from three measurable quantities: the quark scalar gravitational form factor accessible in deeply virtual Compton scattering, the gluon scalar gravitational form factor measurable in near-threshold heavy quarkonium production, and the nucleon sigma-term form factor. We also show that the scalar gluonic form factor extracted from the trace anomaly is quantitatively consistent with lattice QCD and the instanton liquid model over hadronic distance scales. These results provide a direct experimental path to probing the gluonic origin of visible mass.

In light of the great improvement of $ΔN_{\rm eff}$ for the upcoming experiments, we investigate the $Z^\prime$ portal dark matter with Dirac type $ν_R$. In this work, we leverage calorimeter cell-level information to classify highly collimated diphoton signatures, arising from the decay of light axion-like particles, from isolated single-photon showers. Due to the quadratic nature of the coupling, dark matter signals appear at two distinct frequencies: the frequency corresponding to twice the dark matter mass, and frequencies below the typical dark matter kinetic energy. We analyze both contributions and show that LISA can surpass current constraints from terrestrial and astrophysical probes in certain mass ranges. Significant site-dependent differences appear at $E_ν< 10$~GeV, with $ν_μ$ flux at IceCube approximately twice that at JUNO below 1~GeV. Compared to HKKMS15, deviations of 2\%--10\% are attributed to the updated input models. Below 100~MeV, we present precise flux results, revealing that muon propagation contributes a globally significant component to the low-energy neutrino flux at all sites, with an approximately site-independent absolute increment. The hadronic uncertainty is re-estimated across the energy range using the updated hadronic interaction model, with significant reduction of the systematic error compared to previous calculations. These results provide essential inputs for neutrino oscillation and rare-event search experiments including JUNO, Super-Kamiokande/Hyper-Kamiokande, DUNE, KM3NeT/ORCA, and IceCube, as well as direct dark matter detection experiments facing the neutrino fog.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 结合最新中微子振荡数据、CMB和CMB+BAO对中微子质量和的限制、无中微子双贝塔衰变上限以及电子中微子有效质量的运动学限制；对两零纹理进行筛选；对一零纹理采用基于流匹配（flow matching）的机器学习方法进行统计分析；并探讨非可逆选择规则如何导出一零纹理。

Result: 两零纹理中，仅A系列在CMB+BAO强约束下仍可行，B系列在仅CMB约束下可行且预言δ_CP ≈ π/2 或 3π/2；一零纹理中部分已被排除，其余给出∑m_i、m_ν_e^eff、⟨m_ee⟩和δ_CP的明确可区分预测；一零纹理可由非可逆选择规则自然实现。

Conclusion: 中微子质量矩阵的零纹理结构仍具可观测性，尤其是一零纹理在当前数据下仍有生存空间并具备独特可检验预言，其理论起源可通过非可逆对称性机制解释。

Abstract: We revisit one-zero and two-zero textures of the neutrino mass matrix under current experimental and cosmological constraints. We identify the phenomenologically viable texture structures using the latest results on neutrino oscillation parameters, the cosmological bound on the sum of neutrino masses, the kinematic bound on the effective electron-neutrino mass, and limits from neutrinoless double-beta decay. For two-zero textures, several structures are still allowed if only the CMB bound on the neutrino mass sum is imposed. Among them, the $B$-series textures show a characteristic prediction for the Dirac CP phase, with $δ_{\rm CP}$ lying around $π/2$ and $3π/2$, and are within the reach of future neutrinoless double-beta decay searches. When the stronger CMB+BAO constraint is included, however, only the $A$-series textures remain viable. Therefore, we also analyze one-zero textures by using machine learning techniques, particularly flow matching. It turns out that some of the texture structures are already excluded by current data, while the allowed ones give distinct predictions for $\sum_i m_i$, $m_{ν_e}^{\rm eff}$, $\langle m_{ee}\rangle$, and $δ_{\rm CP}$. We further discuss how the one-zero texture structures can arise from non-invertible selection rules.

</details>


### [20] [Electron-Ion Collision Environment: Distribution of Quark Spin and Orbital Angular Momentum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08457)
*Sujit Jana,Ashutosh Dwibedi,Vikash Kumar Ojha,Sabyasachi Ghosh*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 未来电子-离子对撞机（EIC）将能通过eP和eA碰撞测量质子与原子核内相同的部分子分布，从而推动对夸克自旋与轨道角动量在核环境中的理论研究。

Method: 采用有限核密度下的Nambu-Jona-Lasinio（NJL）模型确定零密度与饱和密度下的组分夸克质量，并以此为输入，在光锥 dressed 夸克模型中计算与夸克轨道角动量、自旋及自旋-轨道关联相关的广义横动量依赖部分子分布（GTMDs）；同时引入eP与eA碰撞间的GTMD比值，类比重离子碰撞中的核抑制因子。

Result: 得到了不同核密度下夸克GTMDs的定量结果，并提出GTMD比值偏离1可作为非微扰QCD引起的核多体密度效应的间接探针。

Conclusion: GTMD比值是研究核介质中夸克自旋结构和非微扰QCD效应的有效理论工具，为EIC实验提供关键理论预期与解释框架。

Abstract: The future Electron-Ion Collider (EIC) will enable measurements of the same partonic distributions inside both the proton and the nucleus through electron-proton (eP) and electron-ion (eA) collisions. This capability motivates the present theoretical study of the distributions of quark spin and orbital angular momentum within the proton and the nucleus. To map the eP and eA collision environments, we employ the Nambu--Jona-Lasinio (NJL) model at finite nuclear density to determine the constituent quark masses at zero nuclear density and near the nuclear saturation density. Using these quark mass inputs, we calculate the generalized transverse momentum-dependent parton distributions (GTMDs) associated with quark orbital angular momentum (OAM), spin, and spin-orbit correlations within the light-front dressed quark model. Furthermore, inspired by the nuclear suppression factor widely used in heavy-ion collision experiments, we introduce a set of GTMD ratios between eP and eA collisions. Any deviation of these ratios from unity provides an indirect measure of many-body nuclear density effects arising from non-perturbative quantum chromodynamics (QCD).

### [21] [Leptogenesis and Low Reheating Temperatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08663)
*Marcos A. G. Garcia,Stephen E. Henrich,Wenqi Ke,Keith A. Olive*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了在非瞬时再加热过程中，标准I型跷跷板机制下的轻子生成机制，发现广义Starobinsky势（k≥4）下可在极低再加热温度（高于BBN界限）下成功解释观测到的重子不对称性，且最终重子不对称性主要依赖于两个参数：inflaton-RHN耦合y_φNN和CP破坏参数|ε|，而对RHN质量、再加热温度及衰变速率几乎不敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准轻子生成机制在极低再加热温度下与物质主导再加热（w_φ=0）不兼容，需探索其他再加热动力学以解释观测重子不对称性。

Method: 基于I型跷跷板框架，考虑inflaton衰变（φ→NN）作为右手中微子（RHN）主要非热产生源，分析不同状态方程（w_φ）及广义Starobinsky势（V∝φ^k, k≥4）下的再加热过程，并纳入inflaton凝聚态碎裂效应。

Result: 辐射主导再加热（w_φ=1/3, k=4）下，inflaton有效质量演化导致φ→NN通道运动学关闭，显著改变轻子生成动力学；最终重子不对称性仅强依赖y_φNN和|ε|，对RHN质量、再加热温度和衰变速率几乎不敏感；该结论亦适用于标量玻色子再加热情形。

Conclusion: 广义Starobinsky势（k≥4）支持极低再加热温度下的可行轻子生成，为连接暴胀、再加热与重子不对称性提供了新机制，且参数空间简洁、鲁棒性强。

Abstract: We study leptogenesis during non-instantaneous reheating in the canonical type-I seesaw framework, with the dominant source of right-handed neutrino (RHN) production being non-thermal from inflaton decays ($φ\rightarrow NN$). While matter-like reheating ($w_φ=0$) fails to be compatible with standard leptogenesis for very low reheating temperatures, the situation is strikingly different for generalized Starobinsky potentials approximated by $V(φ)\proptoφ^k$ with $k\geq4$ about the minimum. In the latter cases, the observed baryon asymmetry can readily be obtained for arbitrarily low reheating temperatures above the BBN bound of $\sim4$ MeV. We study radiation-like reheating ($w_φ=1/3$, $k=4$) in detail, showing that the evolving effective mass of the inflaton condensate leads to kinematic shutoff of the $φ\rightarrow NN$ channel, which qualitatively changes the leptogenesis dynamics. We include a detailed treatment of the effects of fragmentation of the inflaton condensate. The final baryon asymmetry depends primarily on only two parameters: the inflaton-RHN coupling, $y_{φNN}$, and the CP-violating parameter $|ε|$. Interestingly, the final asymmetry is largely insensitive to the RHN mass, the reheating temperature, and the RHN decay rate. While we focus on fermionic reheating, we show that the general features of these results also hold for bosonic reheating to scalars.

Abstract: We present a QCD analysis of pion nuclear fragmentation functions (nFFs), which encode nuclear modifications to hadronization in high-energy nuclear collisions. Within this framework, vacuum fragmentation functions and their nuclear modifications are extracted simultaneously. The nuclear effects are parameterized as functions of the mass number $A$, the energy of the fragmenting parton in the target rest frame $ν$, and the hadron energy fraction $z$, allowing their dependence on these variables to be quantified. Our analysis includes semi-inclusive deep-inelastic scattering data on nuclear targets, with kinematic cuts chosen to ensure the applicability of perturbative QCD and collinear factorization. The resulting fit provides a good description of most datasets, with the nFFs well constrained in the energy fraction range $z \in [0.2, 0.7]$.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Negative and pathologically large Monte Carlo event weights strain the computing budgets of experiments at the Large Hadron Collider. Cell resampling algorithms locally redistribute event weights among nearby events in a metric space. We study the performance of metrics defined in terms of Optimal Transport, namely the Energy Mover's Distance and a spectral variant, in the context of such algorithms. As these metrics are insensitive to the addition of soft and collinear radiation, they may be applied directly to particles at any stage of event generation. When applied to samples simulated at next-to-leading-order in quantum chromodynamics, this approach reduces the observed bias relative to other cell resampling techniques presented in the literature. We also study the Cross-Section Mover's Distance as an unbinned, broadly-applicable figure of merit for quantifying the bias introduced by any full-phase-space reweighting.

### [26] [Internal pseudospin, lepton-number superselection, and neutrino--antineutrino coherence in massive neutral-fermion one-particle states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08739)
*Ricardo Romero*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于SU(4)内部对称性的代数框架，用于分类中微子质量类型（Majorana与pseudo-Dirac），通过helicity、电荷共轭及轻子数等算符构造SU(2)伪自旋子代数，并将Majorana条件解释为U₂=+1本征子空间的投影。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为在不预设中微子为Majorana粒子的前提下，统一且代数地刻画中微子质量结构（如neutrinoless double-beta衰变中的ΔL=2过程与active–sterile混合），需超越Wigner小群，构建更普适的内部对称性描述。

Method: 利用四维Dirac中微子单粒子态空间，分析其SU(4)代数结构；识别helicity翻转、电荷共轭及其乘积生成的SU(2)伪自旋子代数；通过泡利矩阵张量积τ_μ⊗σ_ν标记16个生成元，并按轻子数L与helicity ℋ_h分级；将Majorana条件表述为U₂=+1的投影。

Result: 明确了helicity守恒方向（τ_{1,2}⊗σ_{0,3}）对应pseudo-Dirac混合κ_pD，而helicity翻转方向（τ_{1,2}⊗σ_{1,2}）承载无中微子双贝塔衰变的质量项；证实电荷共轭对应U₂生成元，Majorana条件即U₂=+1子空间约束；该框架可不依赖Majorana假设实现质量类型的代数分类。

Conclusion: SU(4)内部伪自旋结构为中微子质量机制提供了新的代数视角，将Majorana性质视为对称性破缺（U₂投影）而非先验假设，从而统一处理active–sterile混合与ΔL=2过程。

Abstract: At fixed three-momentum, massive Dirac neutrino one-particle states span a 4D space of particle--antiparticle identity and helicity. We show that helicity flip, charge conjugation, and their product close an internal $SU(2)$ pseudospin subalgebra within $SU(4)$, distinct from the Wigner little group. Its helicity generator is the lepton-number-weighted spin rotation $U_1=2LJ_2$. The lepton-number $L$ and helicity $\mathcal H_h$ grade the 16 generators $τ_μ\otimesσ_ν$, organizing the $ΔL=2$ sector. Helicity-preserving directions $τ_{1,2}\otimesσ_{0,3}$ carry the pseudo-Dirac mixing $κ_{\rm pD}=Δm^2/4E$ (active--sterile), while helicity-flipping directions $τ_{1,2}\otimesσ_{1,2}$ carry the neutrinoless double-beta decay mass factor (active--active). Furthermore, charge conjugation matches the $U_2$ generator. The Majorana condition is thus a projection onto the $U_2=+1$ eigenspace, where only the Wigner algebra survives. This framework algebraically classifies Majorana masses and pseudo-Dirac splittings without assuming neutrinos are Majorana particles.

</details>

### [27] [Space and Lunar Interferometry: Emerging Concepts and Pathways](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07746)
*Gioia Rau*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Space- and lunar-based interferometry are moving from aspiration toward a concrete landscape of mission studies, pathfinders, and staged architectures. I trace how the science target sets the wavelength regime and angular resolution, which in turn fix the baseline, architecture, and implementation risk. Mid-infrared nulling concepts such as LIFE target temperate exoplanets through thermal-emission spectroscopy; lunar far-side radio arrays (FARSIDE, FarView) open the low-frequency Universe from the only radio-quiet site in the inner Solar System; lunar UV/optical concepts (Artemis-enabled Stellar Imager, MoonLITE) revisit imaging of stellar surfaces and open a path to microarcsecond astrometry for the dynamical masses that Habitable Worlds Observatory target selection requires; far-infrared interferometers (SPIRIT/SPICE), space VLBI (BHEX), and X-ray concepts extend the reach to planet formation, high-redshift galaxies, and black-hole physics; and lunar laser interferometry (LILA) applies the lunar platform to mid-band gravitational waves, measuring strain rather than angular position. Across this range, the concepts share enabling technologies - precision formation flying, absolute metrology, beam combination and nulling, cryogenics, and autonomous deployment - maturing largely as byproducts of flagship programs, a dynamic that increasingly governs which concepts become missions. I summarize the pathways in baseline, wavelength, science return, deployment strategy, and risk, and close with the decisions of the coming decade: pathfinder sequencing, technology tall poles, and the funding models that can carry technologies from laboratory demonstration to flight readiness.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前及未来X射线望远镜灵敏度和光谱分辨率提升，导致弱且混合发射线增多，亟需可重复、系统化的自动识别工具；现有方法多依赖人工或定制化流程，难以实现大样本均一分析。

Method: BLiSS通过直接从观测谱估计经验基线，识别正超出区域，聚类为候选区，用高斯模型表征，并利用高斯混合模型分类器结合合成谱评估候选可靠性；支持多高斯联合拟合与原子跃迁匹配。

Result: 在Chandra/HETGS和XRISM/Resolve对Vela X-1的观测数据上验证了BLiSS性能，成功复现已有主要发射线，具备快速、可重现、仪器无关的探索性谱线搜索能力。

Conclusion: BLiSS是一个模块化、文档完善、公开可用的工具，旨在作为探索性分析手段，补充后续物理谱建模，推动X射线光谱大数据的标准化线识别。

Abstract: The increasing sensitivity and spectral resolution of current and forthcoming X-ray observatories, including \textit{XRISM} and \textit{NewAthena}, are expected to reveal increasing numbers of weak and blended emission lines, motivating reproducible tools for their systematic identification. Existing workflows often rely on manual inspection or source-specific analysis pipelines, making homogeneous analyses of large datasets difficult. To address this need, we present BLiSS (Blind Line Search System), an open-source Python package for the fast, blind detection and characterization of emission-line candidates in one-dimensional X-ray spectra without requiring a prior physical continuum model. BLiSS is intended as an exploratory analysis tool that complements subsequent physical spectral modelling. The package estimates an empirical baseline directly from the observed spectrum, identifies positive excesses, groups them into candidate regions, and characterizes them with Gaussian models. Candidate reliability is estimated by comparison with synthetic spectra using a Gaussian Mixture Model classifier. Finally, optional routines perform a simultaneous multi-Gaussian fit and associate detected features with compatible atomic transitions. The methodology implemented in BLiSS has already enabled published spectroscopic studies and is presented here as a documented, modular, and publicly available software package. Its performance is demonstrated using \textit{Chandra}/HETGS and \textit{XRISM}/Resolve observations of the high-mass X-ray binary Vela X-1, one of the best-studied X-ray sources. BLiSS recovers the principal emission features reported in previous studies while providing a fast, reproducible, and instrument-independent workflow for exploratory line searches.

Method: 构建了包含暗电流去除、拖尾校正和均匀场校正（flat-fielding）的完整辐射定标流程；针对帧转移CCD导致的严重拖尾，设计并实施了严格的校正算法。

Abstract: Danuri, South Korea's first lunar orbiter, was launched on August 5, 2022, and has successfully operated its two-year nominal mission phase. The wide-angle Polarimetric Camera (PolCam) onboard Danuri is the first instrument to conduct global polarimetric observations from lunar orbit. This paper presents the comprehensive radiometric calibration pipeline for PolCam's on-orbit data, consisting of dark current removal, smear correction, and flat-fielding. Notably, PolCam's raw data exhibit severe smear artifacts induced by the frame-transfer CCD architecture, which significantly degrade both radiometric fidelity and the accuracy of polarimetric measurements. These smear artifacts have been effectively mitigated through a rigorous correction algorithm, restoring data quality to a level sufficient for scientific analysis and facilitating the precise derivation of the degree of linear polarization (DoLP). Finally, we present representative examples of polarimetric measurements to validate calibration performance. Although the current calibration focuses on restoring data quality for qualitative scientific analysis, these results clearly demonstrate the expected inverse relationship between intensity and polarization. The absolute photometric calibration required for quantitative DoLP analysis is reserved for a subsequent publication.

### [30] [Catching Disguised Transients with ASTRANet: Anomaly-Aware Spectroscopic Classification and Conformal Calibration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08044)
*Argyro Sasli,Maojie Xu,Alexandra Junell,Hailey Markoff,Avyukt Raghuvanshi,Felipe F. Nunes,Theophile Jegou Du Laz,Jesper Sollerman,Christoffer Fremling,Drew Oldag,Antoine Le Calloch,Sushant Sharma Chaudhary,Sneha Maharjan,Maxine West,Benny Border,Nabeel Rehemtulla,Richard Dekany,Joahan Castaneda Jaimes,Russ R. Laher,Reed Riddle,Mansi M. Kasliwal,Matthew J. Graham,Ashish A. Mahabal,Michael W. Coughlin*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出ASTRANet框架，旨在解决时域巡天中罕见暂现源光谱分类的瓶颈问题，通过分层分类器、异常检测层（ASTRANet-Sentinel）和共形不确定性量化层（ASTRANet-CP），实现对未知类别的光谱进行可信度感知的识别与不确定性校准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统闭集分类器强制将所有输入光谱归入已知类别，无法识别真正属于未知类别的罕见暂现源，限制了物理新发现；亟需一种能区分已知类与未知类并量化置信度的新型分类框架。

Method: 构建ASTRANet三模块框架：1）直接处理观测帧光谱的分层光谱分类器（无需红移或相位先验）；2）基于16种嵌入空间异常分数（涵盖4类物理解释）非线性融合的ASTRANet-Sentinel异常检测层；3）引入AD-stratified Mondrian共形预测（AD-MCP）的ASTRANet-CP不确定性量化层。

Result: 在289个刻意排除于训练集外、涵盖11类罕见/非分类暂现源（如AGN异常、GRB事件、间隙暂现、新星、特殊超新星）的验证集上验证有效；揭示分类器内部不确定性与嵌入式异常检测是互补而非等价的置信度维度；AD-MCP实现异常分数分层下的均匀条件覆盖。

Conclusion: ASTRANet为Vera C. Rubin时代提供了首个系统性、可信度感知的光谱暂现源发现基础设施，突破闭集分类范式，支撑真正未知物理现象的稳健识别与量化评估。

Abstract: Time-domain surveys discover thousands of transients per year, but the spectroscopic identification of rare and physically peculiar objects remains rate-limited by closed-set classifiers that confidently assign every input to a known class -- including spectra that genuinely belong to no known class. We present the \texttt{ASTRANet} framework, a confidence-aware infrastructure for spectroscopic transient classification built around three coupled modules: a hierarchical spectral classifier that operates directly on observer-frame spectra without requiring host-galaxy redshift or spectral phase as inputs; an anomaly detection layer (\texttt{ASTRANet-Sentinel}) that non-linearly combines $16$ embedding-space anomaly scores spanning four physically motivated families; and a conformal uncertainty quantification layer (\texttt{ASTRANet-CP}). We validate the framework on a held-out evaluation set of $289$ rare and out-of-taxonomy transients spanning $11$ classes deliberately excluded from training, chosen to span the full physical diversity of the rare-anomaly population: AGN-related outliers, GRB-related events, gap transients, novae, and peculiar supernovae. Through five astrophysically distinct failure modes of closed-set classifiers, we show that classifier-internal uncertainty and embedding-based anomaly detection are structurally complementary axes of confidence rather than alternative implementations of the same estimator. We further introduce AD-stratified Mondrian conformal prediction (AD-MCP) within \texttt{ASTRANet-CP}, achieving uniform conditional coverage across anomaly-score strata where vanilla Mondrian under-covers in the operational regime. This establishes the methodological infrastructure for confidence-aware spectroscopic discovery in the Vera C.\ Rubin Observatory era.

### [31] [Robust Heteroskedastic Matrix Factorization: A Generalization of PCA that Flags Outliers and Handles Missing Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08081)
*Thomas Hilder,David W. Hogg,Andrew R. Casey,Hans-Walter Rix*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了鲁棒异方差矩阵分解（RHMF），一种推广的PCA方法，能有效处理异常值、特征不确定性及缺失数据，并自动标记特征和对象层面的异常。该方法基于Student-t似然的迭代重加权算法，具有概率层次模型解释，并通过JAX实现高效计算，在天文学光谱数据分析中成功识别出特殊恒星。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统PCA对异常值和不确定性敏感，无法处理缺失数据和特征级不确定性，且缺乏异常检测能力，因此需要一种更鲁棒、更具解释性的降维与异常识别联合方法。

Method: 提出Robust Heteroskedastic Matrix Factorization（RHMF），采用迭代重加权算法最大化Student-t似然，等价于拟合含每个数据点隐变量方差的分层概率模型；提供基于JAX的高效实现Robusta-HMF，并结合交叉验证指导超参选择。

Result: RHMF在多种异常类型下均表现出良好识别与抑制能力；超参数可通过交叉验证可靠设定；在Gaia DR3 RVS光谱数据中成功发现主序星中的异常体，如已知Be星双星系统及显示Ca II三线发射的M矮星（指示吸积或磁活动）。

Conclusion: RHMF是一种兼具鲁棒降维与细粒度异常检测能力的通用方法，适用于含噪声、缺失与不确定性的真实世界高维数据，在天文学等科学领域具有实用价值与可扩展性。

Abstract: We present Robust Heteroskedastic Matrix Factorization (RHMF), a generalization of Principal Component Analysis (PCA) that is robust to outliers, handles per-feature uncertainties and missing data, and automatically flags per-feature and per-object anomalies. RHMF is useful both in recovering a low-dimensional embedding unspoiled by bad data or anomalies, and in identifying those anomalies. It utilises an iterative reweighting algorithm that implicitly maximizes a Student-t likelihood. This admits an equivalent probabilistic interpretation as fitting a hierarchical model with per-data-point latent variances. We deliver a fast JAX implementation, Robusta-HMF, and practical guidance for users. We demonstrate the ability of the model to identify and mitigate outliers of different classes. Identification accuracy is contingent on the choice of hyperparameters, but we show that these can be set reliably by cross-validation. We also apply RHMF to RVS spectra from Gaia DR3 to find main-sequence stars that are strange relative to their neighbors in color-magnitude space. We highlight specific examples, including a known binary hosting a Be star, and M-dwarfs with subtle emission in the Ca II triplet lines, indicative of accretion or magnetic activity, which would not be obvious to identify by eye.

### [32] [On-sky dark hole diggin' with implicit Electric Field Conjugation on MagAO-X](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08146)
*S. Y. Haffert,J. Liberman,J. R. Males,L. M. Close,W. B. Foster,K. Van Gorkom,O. Guyon,A. D. Hedglen,P. T. Johnson,M. Y. Kautz,J. K. Kueny,J. Li,J. D. Long,J. Lumbres,M. Mars,E. A. McEwen,A. McLeod,L. Schatz,E. Tonucci,K. Twitchell*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非共光路像差（NCPA）会通过日冕仪泄漏并产生类似系外行星信号的散斑，严重限制高对比度成像仪器在关键小角距处的探测灵敏度，阻碍对邻近岩石系外行星大气的直接光谱观测。

Method: 利用升级后的MagAO-X仪器（配备专用二级变形镜Kilo-DM）开展焦平面波前传感与控制，采用隐式电场共轭（iEFC）算法，并基于内部光源标定交互矩阵，实现星上实时NCPA校正。

Result: 在HR4796A和南门二等目标上、0.5角秒视宁度条件下，成功实现星上NCPA校正，抑制因子达2–20倍；验证了离线标定与星上对准的一致性及iEFC算法在真实观测条件下的鲁棒性与高效性。

Conclusion: 该工作证实iEFC结合专用二级AO系统可有效解决NCPA问题，为极大望远镜（ELT）和巨型麦哲伦望远镜（GMT）等下一代AO系统集成提供了关键技术支撑。

Abstract: Direct spectroscopy is very promising approach to characterizing the atmospheres of nearby rocky exoplanets. Non-common path aberrations (NCPA) are differential aberrations between the science optical path and the adaptive optics optical path. The NCPA leak through the coronagraph and create speckles that mimic exoplanet signals. This limits the sensitivity of high-contrast imaging instruments at close angular separations - exactly the separations where we want to search for rocky exoplanets with current and future telescopes and instruments. We aim to actively remove the NCPA on-sky during observations by using focal plane wavefront sensing and control with the newly upgraded MagAO-X instrument. MagAO-X is equipped with a unique second-stage Adaptive Optics (AO) system. The second-stage AO system contains a dedicated deformable mirror (DM) for coronagraphic focal plane wavefront control. This DM is placed after the science and AO beam-splitter and is therefore not seen by the main AO loop. The DM has been recently upgraded from an ALPAO-97 to a Boston Micromachine Kilo-DM. The new Kilo-DM enables focal plane wavefront control with the implicit Electric Field Conjugation (iEFC) algorithm. We developed the necessary procedures to run iEFC with MagAO-X on-sky. We demonstrated the successful removal of NCPA on-sky with an iEFC interaction matrix that was calibrated on the MagAO-X internal source. This demonstrates the repeatability between our off-sky and on-sky alignment. The iEFC algorithm was tested on HR4796A and Alpha Centauri in 0.5" seeing conditions. We saw a reduction of the NCPA by a factor of 2 to 20. This on-sky validation confirms the robustness and efficiency of iEFC under realistic observing conditions, paving the way for its integration into next-generation AO systems for the Extremely Large Telescope and Giant Magellan Telescope.

### [36] [DegenDetector: Symbolic Recovery of Parameter Degeneracies in Bayesian Posteriors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08755)

Conclusion: DegenDetector 弥合了相关性可视化与函数形式发现之间的鸿沟，为统计建模与科学解释提供了新的可解释性工具。

Abstract: We introduce DegenDetector, a framework for identifying and characterizing parameter degeneracies in posterior distributions as closed-form symbolic equations. By combining mutual information screening with alternating symbolic regression, we facilitate automated and interpretable identification of degenerate relationships without domain-specific input. While standard tools such as corner plots can indicate that correlations exist, they do not reveal the underlying functional form. DegenDetector fills this gap by expressing multi-parameter degeneracies as closed-form equations, providing interpretable structure that scales to high-order parameter spaces.

</details>

### [37] [Quantization of Gravity on Null Hypersurfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07785)
*Luca Ciambelli,Marc S. Klinger*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文构建了广义相对论特征初值问题（CIVP）的算子代数量子化方案，利用角对称性分别量子化两个相交的类光超曲面，并在共同的二维角处粘合，所得代数包含超平移、超旋转和超 boosts 的内作用，其中超平移被实现为量子信道而非代数自同构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 类光超曲面上的广义相对论柯西问题（即特征初值问题CIVP）物理内涵丰富但尚未被充分量子化，尤其需要处理两个类光超曲面在二维角处的数据拼接及相应对称性结构。

Method: 基于角对称性分别对每个类光超曲面进行量子化，再在共享的二维角处粘合；将超平移量子化为量子信道，借助广义Stinespring扩张定理纳入代数；超 boosts 和超旋转则用于实现爱因斯坦方程所导出的引力约束。

Result: 得到一个具有完整角对称（半）群（含超 boosts、超旋转、超平移）内作用的量子代数，其中超平移以量子信道形式实现；该代数可作为局部无焦散区域内一对类光超曲面所张成引力子区域的壳上代数候选。

Conclusion: 本文首次实现了CIVP的算子代数量子化，揭示了角对称性在引力子区域量子代数构造中的核心作用，为黑洞信息、边界理论与全息原理提供了新的代数框架。

Abstract: The initial value problem for general relativity on spacelike hypersurfaces is famously captured by the ADM formalism. Less well known is the Cauchy problem for general relativity on null hypersurfaces, which goes under the name of the Characteristic Initial Value Problem (CIVP). The CIVP is formulated on a pair of intersecting null hypersurfaces, encoding rich physics in the interplay between their respective initial data, and especially the gluing of these hypersurfaces at their shared codimension-two corner. In this work, we construct an operator-algebraic quantization of the CIVP. To do so, we first quantize each null hypersurface separately, using the corner symmetries as a guiding principle, and then glue them together at the joint initial cut. The resulting algebra admits an inner action of the full corner symmetry (semi)group consisting of superboosts, superrotations, and supertranslations. These are associated, respectively, with the quantization of the area, the Hájiček one-form, and the expansion along both null directions. Supertranslations do not act as algebra preserving maps, but instead are quantized to quantum channels and included into the algebra via a generalized form of the Stinespring dilation theorem. The inclusion of superboosts and superrotations implements the gravitational constraints arising from Einstein's equations at the level of the quantum algebra. By virtue of the CIVP, in its local caustic-free domain of validity, our construction yields a candidate for the on-shell algebra of a gravitational subregion subtended by a pair of null hypersurfaces.

</details>


### [38] [Gram--Wishart--Stiefel formulation of the $N=2$, large--$d$ gauge theory in 1D](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08481)
*Badis Ydri*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文发展了BFSS/BMN矩阵量子力学在大维数d下的平面端点理论的Gram/Wishart/Stiefel表述，通过重新组织端点自由度为Wishart特征值与Stiefel角变量，实现了对全息势中A、B及R²等不变量的直接分析；关键发现是大R对齐渐近下全息势的普适线性项−A被吸收到高斯部分，导致有效质量参数偏移，并由秩二Bessel核精确编码；进一步应用该结构于横向B型展开及其非多项式玩具补全，证明了有限多项式截断所导致的大d微扰性界限实为截断伪影，最终恢复物理的Wishart鞍点并重现DΛ通道的普适−2d贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为理解BFSS/BMN矩阵模型在大维数极限下的全息结构与连续统行为，需克服传统笛卡尔变量在分析全息不变量（如A、B、R²）时的局限性，建立能自然分离径向与角自由度的新变量框架。

Method: 引入Gram/Wishart/Stiefel变量重构端点自由度；利用大R对齐渐近分析全息势；通过精确O(2)角积分导出秩二Bessel核以编码有效质量偏移；结合横向B型展开与非多项式补全，系统处理截断误差并恢复物理鞍点。

Result: 确立了Gram/Wishart/Stiefel变量下全息势的精确结构，揭示了−A项导致的有效质量偏移(α_Λ)_eff=α_Λ−1/2；证明有限B型多项式截断的微扰性界限为伪影；成功恢复物理Wishart鞍点，并复现D_Λ通道的普适−2d连续统贡献。

Conclusion: Gram/Wishart/Stiefel表述为大d矩阵量子力学提供了更本质的几何与统计视角，不仅统一处理全息不变量，且澄清了横向展开中截断效应与真实连续统行为之间的区别，为后续研究各向异性β_Λ通道奠定基础。

Abstract: We develop in this paper the Gram/Wishart/Stiefel formulation of the \(N=2\), large--\(d\) planar endpoint theory of the BFSS/BMN matrix quantum mechanics on the lattice, obtained in our previous work. In this formulation, the endpoint degrees of freedom are reorganized into rank--two Wishart eigenvalues and relative Stiefel angular variables. This allows the holonomy invariants \(A\), \(B\), and \(R^2=A^2+B^2\) to be analyzed directly in terms of radial and angular Gram data.
  A central point is the large-\(R\) aligned asymptotics of the holonomy potential. Its universal linear contribution \(-A\) is absorbed into the Gaussian sector, producing the shifted mass parameter
  \((α_Λ)_{\rm eff}=α_Λ-1/2\). In the Gram/Wishart/Stiefel variables, the exact \(O(2)\) angular integral encodes this shifted sector in a rank--two Bessel kernel. The pure \(-A\) theory, which is exactly solvable in Cartesian variables, then fixes the leading Bessel/HCIZ structure: its exponential part selects the aligned configuration, while its prefactor removes the spurious doubled Wishart entropy.
  We then apply this structure to the transverse \(B\)-type expansion and its non-polynomial toy completion. Finite polynomial truncations lead to an apparent large--\(d\) perturbativity bound incompatible with the continuum limit, but this bound is shown to be an artifact of truncation. After summing the local transverse completion and balancing the compensating \(+A\) term, the Wishart saddle is recovered with the physical shifted mass. The resulting continuum behavior reproduces the universal \(-2d\) contribution of the \(D_Λ\)-channel, while the genuinely anisotropic \(β_Λ\)-channel lies outside the scope of a pure transverse \(B\)-type description.

</details>


### [39] [Chiral Tube Algebras I: Topological Defect Lines, Twisted Modules, and Finite Gauging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07786)
*Nathan Benjamin,Ho Tat Lam,Conghuan Luo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文引入了手性管代数（chiral tube algebras），统一并推广了二维共形场论中手性代数与拓扑缺陷线（TDLs）两种对称性描述，使其能处理扭曲缺陷希尔伯特空间及非局域手性流，并适用于有限gauging后的对称性结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性代数和拓扑缺陷线（TDLs）是二维共形场论中两种互补的对称性概念，但缺乏统一框架；尤其在有限gauging后，原有手性代数可能生成非局域流，需新结构来刻画。

Method: 提出手性管代数：扩展手性代数作用范围至TDL扭曲的缺陷希尔伯特空间，并允许由TDL附着的非局域手性流，从而实现不同缺陷空间间的映射；结合Kac-Moody、W代数、超共形代数及其orbifold/bosonization等实例构造不可约模。

Result: 构建了手性管代数及其不可约模（同构于对应手性代数的扭曲模），用以系统组织局域与缺陷希尔伯特空间；为gauging后手性结构提供自然描述框架；为后续研究分数自旋非局域手性流奠定基础。

Conclusion: 手性管代数成功统一手性对称性与拓扑缺陷结构，拓展了传统手性代数的适用范围，成为研究2d CFT中广义对称性（尤其是gauging与非局域流）的有力新工具。

Abstract: Chiral algebras and topological defect lines (TDLs) represent two complementary notions of symmetry in 2d conformal field theories. In this paper, we introduce chiral tube algebras to unify and extend these two notions. Chiral tube algebras generalize chiral algebras in two ways. First, they extend the action of chiral algebras beyond the local Hilbert space to include defect Hilbert spaces twisted by TDLs. Second, they allow for non-local chiral currents attached by TDLs and thus can map between different defect Hilbert spaces, analogous to the tube algebras of TDLs. Since local chiral currents can become non-local after finite gauging, chiral tube algebras provide a natural framework for describing the image of chiral algebras under such gauging. We illustrate this framework through a variety of examples that generalize familiar chiral algebras, including Kac-Moody algebras, $\mathcal{W}$ algebras, superconformal algebras, and their orbifolds/bosonizations. We construct their irreducible modules, which are isomorphic to twisted modules of the corresponding chiral algebras, and use them to organize local and defect Hilbert spaces. In a subsequent paper, we will study chiral tube algebras generated by non-local chiral currents with fractional spins, which have no counterparts in chiral algebras.

Conclusion: 量子聚焦猜想的Rényi推广不成立，揭示了其与经典量子信息结构之间的深刻限制。

Abstract: The quantum focusing conjecture is a mathematical expression of the idea that semiclassical gravity remains universally attractive. Its off-diagonal part is a monotonicity condition on the double null shape variation of relative entropy on distinct null generators, and has been argued to follow from strong subadditivity of entanglement entropy. Recent proof of a diagonal Rényi quantum null energy condition raises the question: does a full Rényi focusing statement also hold? We answer this question negatively for any Rényi-type divergence satisfying data processing, tensor additivity, and matched classical--quantum conditioning.

### [41] [Relative entropy for $λφ^4$ in the Rindler wedge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07810)
*Markus B. Fröb,Albert Much,Kyriakos Papadopoulos*

TL;DR: 本文计算了相互作用λφ⁴理论中Rindler楔形区域内真空态与相干态之间的相对熵（至λ的一阶），利用Tomita-Takesaki模理论和Araki-Uhlmann公式，验证其等于经典（相互作用）提升Noether荷，并满足Bekenstein界限。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建Rindler楔形区域的微扰相互作用Weyl代数，结合Tomita-Takesaki模理论与Araki-Uhlmann公式计算相对熵。

Result: 相对熵在λ一阶下精确等于经典提升Noether荷；Bekenstein界限依然成立。

Conclusion: 即使在弱相互作用下，Rindler楔形中真空与相干态的相对熵仍具有清晰的几何/热力学解释，支持全息与黑洞热力学的基本结构在相互作用理论中的稳健性。

Abstract: We consider the relative entropy between the vacuum and a coherent state in the Rindler wedge for an interacting $λφ^4$ theory to first order in $λ$. We construct the perturbatively interacting Weyl algebra of the wedge, and employ Tomita--Takesaki modular theory and the Araki--Uhlmann formula to compute the relative entropy. We verify that the relative entropy reduces to the classical (interacting) boost Noether charge, analogously to the free theory, and that the Bekenstein bound holds.

### [42] [The Energy-Momentum-News Complex near Future Null Infinity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07872)

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了三维和四维渐近平直真空爱因斯坦解在将来零无穷远处的几何结构，引入Carroll协变Bondi-Sachs规范，构建了边界能量-动量-新闻复形，并导出其满足的Ward型恒等式及Carroll协变的Bondi能量损失方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解渐近平直时空在零无穷远处的几何结构及其对称性，特别是Carroll几何在引力边界理论中的作用。

Method: 采用Carroll协变的Bondi-Sachs规范，从一般Carroll边界数据出发求解爱因斯坦方程，并通过重整化作用量变分定义边界能量-动量-新闻复形，分析其在边界微分同胚、Weyl变换和Carroll提升下的对称性与反常。

Result: 推导出边界能量-动量-新闻复形满足的三个Ward型恒等式（其中Carroll提升对应的为反常关系），并由此得到Carroll协变形式的Bondi能量损失方程。

Conclusion: Carroll几何为描述零无穷处边界结构提供了自然框架，边界对称性及其反常深刻影响能量输运与守恒律的形式。

Abstract: We study asymptotically flat vacuum solutions of general relativity in three and four dimensions, with an emphasis on the geometric structures that emerge near null infinity. We construct asymptotic solutions to the three- and four-dimensional Einstein equations near future null infinity, which is a conformal Carroll manifold, starting from the most general Carroll metric data allowed by the Einstein equations. We use a Carroll-covariant version of Bondi--Sachs gauge, whose residual transformations act on the boundary Carroll geometry and shear as boundary diffeomorphisms, Weyl transformations and Carroll boosts. We then define a boundary energy-momentum-news complex at future null infinity by varying a suitably renormalised action with respect to the boundary Carroll metric data and shear. This involves adding boundary terms to the Einstein--Hilbert action on a cut-off surface near future null infinity. The boundary energy-momentum-news complex obeys two relations due to the boundary diffeomorphism and Weyl gauge invariance of the renormalised action. A third relation, due to the Carroll boost, is anomalous, and the corresponding anomaly is obtained from the variation of the renormalised action. Together, these Ward-type identities obeyed by the boundary energy-momentum-news complex lead to a Carroll-covariant generalisation of the Bondi loss equations.

Abstract: We study generalized global symmetries of the bosonic M2-brane in eleven-dimensional backgrounds with non-trivial four-form flux. Motivation: 研究Carrollian极限在超引力理论中的实现，以深化对低速（无限光速）极限下对称性与场论结构的理解。

Result: 明确得到了四维N=1超引力的电与磁Carrollian极限理论；该方法可自然延拓至更一般的扩展超引力情形。

Conclusion: Carrollian超引力存在两种互补的极限实现方式，为Carroll对称性量子场论及非相对论超对称性研究提供了新框架。

Abstract: The electric and magnetic carrollian limits of $N=1$ supergravity in $D=4$ spacetime dimensions are explicitly derived. The approach is general and applies also to extended supergravity models

</details>


### [48] [Gauge-Invariant Off-Shell Mass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08426)
*Kang-Sin Choi,Hyeseon Im*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种规范不变且可重整化的离壳质量函数，通过推广捏合技术（pinch technique）到任意长的费米子线，结合局域Ward-Takahashi恒等式，消除了自能中的规范依赖项，得到费曼规范下的自能；该方法导出的质量函数规范不变、方案无关，并在壳值等于物理质量，同时其标量部分红外有限，可与Dyson-Schwinger方程和格点计算结果直接比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统自能在离壳时具有规范依赖性，限制了其物理意义和应用；需构造一个规范不变、过程无关、可直接与非微扰方法（如Dyson-Schwinger方程和格点QCD）比较的离壳质量定义。

Method: 将捏合技术推广至任意长费米子线，结合每个顶点处局域作用的Ward-Takahashi恒等式，精确抵消规范依赖项，从而构造出规范不变的广义自能和顶点函数；在此基础上进行壳上重整化。

Result: 得到一个规范不变、方案无关的离壳质量函数，其壳上值等于物理质量；对应的标量自能红外有限，可直接与Schwinger-Dyson方程和格点模拟结果对比；该构造在任意多光子外线的振幅中每段内费米子线上均成立，并通过最小离壳康普顿振幅验证。

Conclusion: 本文成功构建了严格规范不变且物理可解释的离壳质量概念，为微扰与非微扰方法之间建立了桥梁，增强了对强耦合区质量动力学的理解。

Abstract: We define a gauge-invariant and renormalized off-shell mass function in quantum field theory. The conventional self-energy is gauge-dependent off-shell. We generalize the self-energy, together with the corresponding vertex function, to be gauge-invariant and process-independent. To do this, we extend the pinch technique to an arbitrarily long fermion line. The Ward-Takahashi identity acting locally at each vertex cancels the gauge-dependent piece exactly, leaving the Feynman-gauge self-energy. On-shell renormalization then yields a mass function that is gauge-invariant, scheme-independent and equal to the physical mass at the pole; the same self-energy also yields an infrared-finite scalar mass function directly comparable with Schwinger-Dyson and lattice determinations. The cancellation is local to the internal fermion line and holds entirely off-shell, so the self-energy is well-defined on each internal segment of an amplitude with arbitrarily many external photons; we demonstrate this explicitly by computing the minimal off-shell Compton amplitude.

</details>

Method: 基于三维拓扑质量引力（含引力Chern–Simons项），采用Newman–Penrose形式分析BTZ与扭曲BTZ黑洞的一圈效应；对比近视界计算与全几何本征值问题；考察Schwarzian与旋转模在小温度下的抬升行为。

Result: 发现旋转模对BTZ与扭曲BTZ黑洞的近极值热力学至关重要，不能随意忽略，其处理必须结合具体边界条件；明确了Schwarzian与旋转 sector 在小温度下的量子抬升机制。

Conclusion: 在近极值黑洞的量子分析中，旋转自由度不可简化或忽略，其物理意义依赖于边界条件；该结论对理解极值黑洞微观结构与低能有效理论具有重要启示。

Abstract: We study one-loop effects in the near-extremal thermodynamics of BTZ and warped BTZ black holes, with particular emphasis on the fate of eigenmodes that become zero modes in the extremal throat. Our analysis is formulated in three-dimensional Topologically Massive Gravity, a higher derivative theory characterized by the presence of a gravitational Chern--Simons term, and it makes use of the Newman--Penrose formulation. For BTZ, we compare the near-horizon computation with the full-geometry eigenvalue problem and identify how the Schwarzian and rotational sectors are lifted at small temperature. We then extend the same strategy to warped BTZ. We find that rotational modes are essential for a consistent near-extremal treatment of both BTZ and warped BTZ black holes, and cannot be discarded without first specifying the boundary conditions.

### [50] [The Remnant of an Evaporating Rotating Regular Black Hole from the Generalized Entropy in the Final Stage of Evaporation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08661)
*Shingo Takeuchi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了旋转正则黑洞在蒸发末期霍金辐射的广义熵，通过将黑洞质量表示为极值质量与参数α之和，发现当修正项消失时α存在有限下界α₁，表明黑洞蒸发会留下质量为m_ext+α₁的残余物。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在黑洞蒸发末期，中心区域的精细结构变得重要，因此采用正则化处理；同时考虑旋转黑洞以增强结论的普适性。

Method: 将黑洞质量表示为m_ext+α，分析广义熵中面积项与修正项的符号不变性，并确定使修正项消失的α下界。

Result: 发现修正项消失时的α具有有限下界α₁，意味着黑洞质量不能低于m_ext+α₁，即蒸发末期将产生残余物。

Conclusion: 旋转正则黑洞在蒸发末期会形成具有有限质量的残余物，这为解决信息悖论和黑洞终极命运提供了新视角。

Abstract: We express the generalized entropy (GE) of the Hawking radiation in the final stage of an evaporating rotating regular black hole (BH) by writing the mass of the BH as $m_{\rm ext}+α$, where $m_{\rm ext}$ represents the mass at the extremal limit and $α$ is a parameter. Generally, entropy is non-negative. Based on this fact, we assume that, in the GE considered in this study, the signs of the contributions from the area term and the correction term remain unchanged throughout the entire evaporation process of the BH. Therefore, we regard $α$ at which the correction term vanishes as its lower bound and determine it. As a result, we find that such a value of $α$ is finite. Denoting this value by $α_1$, this result indicates that the mass of the BH cannot become smaller than $m_{\rm ext}+α_1$, which can be interpreted as the emergence of a remnant at the final stage of BH evaporation. The BH considered in this study is a rotating regular BH. The regularization is motivated by the fact that the fine structure of the central region becomes relevant in the final stage of evaporation. A rotating BH is considered from the viewpoint of generality.

### [51] [Entanglement Wedge Reconstruction without Holographic Quantum Error Correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08684)
*Seiji Terashima*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文讨论AdS/CFT中体空间重构问题，指出子区域重构（即纠缠楔重构）不应被等同于更强的全息量子纠错解释；后者要求一个与区域无关的逻辑体算符在多个边界区域中有保持编码的表示。作者论证，在有限N的全息CFT中并不存在这种全息量子纠错，因为低能局域可观测量（如适当涂抹的应力张量）可探测普通体算符的物理支撑与引力修饰，故不存在‘受保护的不可见子系统’。因此，体空间重构应理解为子区域互补性：每个边界子区域拥有自身保持编码的低能代数及相应适配的体空间诠释，而非共享逻辑算符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清AdS/CFT中体空间重构的本质，特别是区分纠缠楔重构与全息量子纠错这两种常被混用的概念，并指出后者在真实有限N全息CFT中不成立。

Method: 基于局域性论证，分析代码保持算符代数在互补区域上的对易关系；结合HaPPY类码的结构与有限N全息CFT中低能可观测量（如应力张量）的行为进行对比论证。

Result: 证明有限N全息CFT中不存在全息量子纠错所需的受保护不可见逻辑代数；HKLL公式在N→∞时全局与子区域结果一致仅适用于自由场论；真正的体空间重构应理解为子区域互补性。

Conclusion: 纠缠楔重构无需依赖全息量子纠错框架；应放弃‘共享逻辑算符’图景，转而接受每个边界子区域具有独立、适配的低能代数与体空间诠释。

Abstract: Bulk reconstruction is a central problem in AdS/CFT, and entanglement wedge reconstruction is its subregion version. We argue that this subregion statement should be separated from the stronger holographic quantum error correction interpretation, in which one region-independent logical bulk operator has code-preserving representatives in several boundary regions. A simple locality argument shows that such a common reconstruction must commute with the code-preserving local algebras in the complementary regions. This is the mechanism realized in HaPPY-type codes: the erased regions are blind to a protected logical algebra. An ordinary finite $N$ holographic CFT does not have such a protected invisible sector for supergravity fields. Its low-energy local observables, in particular, suitably smeared stress tensors, detect the physical support and gravitational dressing of ordinary bulk operators, up to possible center or superselection data. Thus, there is no such holographic quantum error correction and the $N=\infty$ agreement of global and subregion HKLL formulae is a free-theory statement. What remains is entanglement wedge reconstruction without holographic quantum error correction, or subregion complementarity: each boundary region has its own code-preserving low-energy algebra and its own region-adapted bulk interpretation, rather than a shared logical operator.

</details>


### [52] [The mini-Page Curve in Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08737)
*Ricardo Espíndola,Shoichiro Miyashita*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了德西特宇宙视界中霍金对携带量子信息逃逸的时间点，通过构建二维流形几何模型和代数方法，发现信息逃逸始于约τ≈β/8时刻，并揭示了其与纠缠楔广义熵及李雅普诺夫指数的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞信息悖论激发了对蒸发黑洞中信息逃逸机制的研究，本文旨在探讨类似问题在宇宙学视界（特别是德西特视界）中的表现，即霍金对何时开始携带信息离开视界。

Method: 构建一类连接渐近AdS₂边界与dS₂静态补丁的二维流形几何；用局域算符及其模共轭构造探测态模拟霍金对发射；通过叉积构造将半人马代数提升为II∞型因子；计算热场双重态与霍金对态之间的熵差；推广至微正则系综并关联纠缠楔广义熵；分析相对模流以提取李雅普诺夫指数。

Result: 熵差呈现特征性的微型Page曲线：起始接近零，在τ≈β/8处达最小值后上升；该最小值位置被解释为量子信息开始逃逸宇宙学视界的时间；代数熵与纠缠楔广义熵一致；相对模流给出李雅普诺夫指数λ=2π/β，对应信息对静态补丁观测者变得可访问的混沌时间尺度（即扰乱时间）。

Conclusion: 德西特宇宙视界的信息逃逸具有明确的时间标度（τ≈β/8），其动力学可通过代数量子场论与全息熵框架统一描述，表明宇宙学视界亦遵循类似黑洞的信息释放规律。

Abstract: The black hole information paradox has motivated extensive study of how and when information escapes from evaporating black holes. Here we address the analogous question for cosmological horizons: when does an individual Hawking pair begin to carry information out of a de Sitter horizon? We study this problem in a class of two-dimensional flow geometries that interpolate smoothly between an asymptotic AdS$ _2 $ boundary and a dS$ _2 $ static patch. Modeling the emission of a Hawking pair via a probe state constructed from local operators and their modular conjugates, we promote the centaur algebra of observables to a Type II$ _\infty $ factor through the crossed-product construction. This allows us to compute the entropy difference between the thermofield-double reference state and the Hawking-pair state. We find that this difference traces a characteristic mini-Page curve for the cosmological horizon: it starts near zero, reaches a minimum near $ τ\approx β/8 $ before increasing again. We interpret the location of the minimum as the time at which quantum information begins to escape the cosmological horizon. Extending the analysis to the microcanonical ensemble, we show that the algebraic entropy coincides with the generalized entropy of an entanglement wedge cut that tracks the emitted particle along the horizon. Furthermore, the relative modular flow generated between the two states yields a Lyapunov exponent $λ=2π/β$, identifying the scrambling time as the scale at which the information carried by the pair becomes accessible to a static-patch observer.

*Peng Yang,Kilar Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究极端带电C度规的角本征值问题，发现其控制微分方程在极端极限下退化为合流扩展Heun方程，并借助四维N=2线性quiver规范理论中的去耦极限，结合瞬子计数方法导出满足边界条件的代数量子化条件，从而解析获得角本征值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解极端带电C-metric中角向波动方程的本征谱，尤其在Q→M极限下因奇点融合导致方程退化所带来的解析困难。

Method: 将角向方程映射到四维N=2、SU(2)×SU(2)线性quiver规范理论的去耦极限；建立参数字典与重整化Matone关系以吸收奇点融合引起的宏观留数偏移；利用瞬子计数方法结合正则边界条件推导代数量子化条件。

Result: 成功解析求得角本征值，结果与数值计算一致；揭示了引力角向问题与规范理论间深刻的对偶联系。

Abstract: We investigate the angular eigenvalue problem of the extreme charged C-metric. In the extreme limit ($Q \to M$), the governing differential equation degenerates from a Fuchsian equation with five regular singular points into a Confluent Extended Heun Equation. To evaluate the angular spectrum analytically, we formulate a decoupling limit within the dual four-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=2$, $\mathrm{SU(2)}\times \mathrm{SU(2)}$ linear quiver gauge theory. Within this framework, we derive the parameter dictionary and renormalized Matone relations, which absorb the macroscopic residue shifts induced by the singularity fusion. Based on the regular boundary conditions of the angular equation, we utilize the instanton counting method to establish an algebraic quantization condition, yielding angular eigenvalues consistent with numerical results.

### [54] [Phase-dependent kink collisions and dual critical-velocity branches in the complex sine-Gordon model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08752)
*Mohammad Mohammadi,Farnaz Eizadbaksh,Vahideh Bagheri*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，系统扫描不同初始速度与相对相位组合下的复kink-kink碰撞过程，分析终态类型、辐射能量、中心点能量密度及场模等物理量。

Result: 发现两种相位依赖的临界速度分支：一支中增大初速促进捕获，另一支则恢复散射；各诊断量在临界点呈现尖锐跃变；相对相位作为有效内禀自由度主导碰撞结果。

Abstract: The complex sine-Gordon (CSG) model contains an internal phase degree of freedom that strongly modifies the dynamics of its solitary-wave solutions. We present a numerical study of complex kink--kink collisions and determine how the final state depends jointly on the initial velocity and relative phase. In contrast with the elastic collisions of the real sine-Gordon model, the CSG system exhibits scattering, capture, long-lived bion formation, breather-like states, and emission of radiative profiles. The simulations reveal two distinct phase-dependent branches of critical velocity. In one branch, increasing the initial velocity promotes capture, whereas in the other it restores scattering. This dual structure highlights the rich velocity--phase dependence of the collision dynamics. We also compute the energy carried by radiative profiles and examine extreme values of the energy density, kinetic and gradient contributions, and field modulus at the collision center. These quantities show sharp transitions at critical points and provide sensitive diagnostics of phase-controlled dynamics. These results suggest that the relative phase behaves as an effective internal degree of freedom that plays an important role in the collision dynamics of complex solitons.

### [55] [Infrared-enhanced Photometric Redshifts for the Dark Energy Survey Y6 Gold catalogue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07771)
*M. M. Puebla,I. Sevilla-Noarbe,J. de Vicente,L. Toribio San Cipriano,J. Carretero,A. Drlica-Wagner,J. García-Bellido,D. Gruen,J. Gschwend,T. A. Manning,M. de la Osa,A. Porredon,N. Reynes,E. Sánchez,P. Tallada,N. Weaverdyck*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了将DES光学数据与VHS和WISE红外数据结合以提升光度红移（photo-z）估计精度的效果，发现WISE数据（尤其是W1/W2波段）显著改善了photo-z性能，而VHS数据在当前深度下贡献有限，低信噪比红外数据无额外增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用DES光学数据与红外巡天（VHS和WISE）结合，提升光度红移估计精度，并发布更新星表。

Method: 通过位置交叉匹配DES Y6 Gold星表、光谱数据集、AllWISE 2013版和VHS DR5，采用DNF算法评估photo-z性能；并用unWISE验证。

Result: 加入WISE数据显著降低photo-z的散度、偏差和异常值比例，尤其在高红移区；VHS数据提升微弱；z<1.5时VHS无额外改进；信噪比<10的红外数据无改善作用。

Conclusion: WISE W1/W2数据已足够提供准确photo-z所需的关键红外信息和深度，当前深度下VHS及低信噪比红外数据无实质性贡献。

Abstract: The Dark Energy Survey (DES) provides optical data across 5000 square degrees of the southern sky, enabling a broad range of extragalactic and cosmological studies. Combining DES data with infrared surveys offers the opportunity to improve its photometric redshift (photo-z) estimates. We aim to investigate improvements in photometric redshift estimation achieved by combining DES optical data with infrared measurements from the VISTA Hemisphere Survey (VHS) and the Wide-field Infrared Survey Explorer (WISE), and release an updated version of the catalogue. We performed a positional sky cross-match between the DES Y6 Gold catalogue matched to a spectroscopic dataset, the 2013 AllWISE Data Release, and VHS Data Release 5, in order to test these improvements using the Directional Neighbourhood Fitting (DNF) algorithm (Y6 Gold catalogue reference estimator). We additionally matched it to the unWISE catalogue to verify the performance against this deeper dataset. Adding infrared data reduces all the metrics (scatter, bias and outlier fraction) in photo-z estimates, particularly at higher redshifts in comparison with only using optical data from DES. The obtained results are globally better for the DES+WISE sample, with improvements that are statistically significant. On the other hand, the addition of the VHS bands to available depth is only marginal. The combined use of DES and WISE W1 and W2 data improves the photometric redshift metrics analysed here. The addition of VHS data at the DES and VHS depths explored here does not provide any further improvement at z less than 1.5, indicating that, under these constraints, WISE data may already capture the key infrared features and depth needed for accurate photo-z estimation. In addition, low signal-to-noise (less than 10) infrared data does not contribute to any improvement beyond the DES optical dataset.

*Carlos García-García,Pedro G. Ferreira,William J. Wolf*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文评估了单标量场暗能量模型的当前观测状态，指出尽管动力学标量场（如精质）可解释宇宙加速膨胀，但其与宇宙常数Λ仍难以区分；EFT扩展模型虽有微弱统计偏好，但受数据选择和先验影响显著，并面临第五力、结构增长及天体物理约束等挑战；ISW效应与增长速率观测目前一致，但未来Stage IV巡天仍难彻底解决参数欠定问题，最终验证依赖于低红移结构增长测量与引力屏蔽机制的理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受近期宇宙学观测（BAO、Ia型超新星、CMB）驱动，检验单标量场模型能否作为暗能量的可行解释。

Method: 基于有效场论（EFT）框架，结合当前多源宇宙学观测数据（BAO、SNe Ia、CMB、ISW、结构增长速率、太阳系实验），分析参数约束能力、模型区分度及理论可行性（如第五力、筛选机制）。

Result: 精质模型与Λ仅边缘可区分；EFT扩展模型统计偏好微弱且不稳定；预测的第五力与结构增长修改面临强天体物理约束；当前ISW与增长数据彼此一致；Stage IV巡天将提升约束但无法消除欠定性。

Conclusion: 单标量场暗能量仍是自然灵活的框架，但其最终有效性取决于低红移结构增长的更精确测量及引力筛选机制的理论与观测进展。

Abstract: We present an assessment of the current observational status of single scalar field models of dark energy. Motivated by recent cosmological measurements -- including baryon acoustic oscillations, Type Ia supernovae, and CMB data -- we examine whether a dynamical scalar field offers a viable explanation for the accelerated expansion of the Universe. Working within an effective field theory (EFT) framework, we argue that cosmological observations are fundamentally limited and can at most constrain a small number of parameters that govern scalar field dynamics. We show that quintessence remains only marginally distinguishable from a cosmological constant, $Λ$, and that more general EFT extensions exhibit modest statistical preference, though such evidence is sensitive to data set selection and prior assumptions. These extended models generically predict fifth forces and modifications to the growth of structure, raising challenges from astrophysical constraints. We compare their predictions with current growth rate measurements, Integrated Sachs-Wolfe (ISW) effect and Solar System constraints. We emphasize that viable screening mechanisms remain theoretically non-trivial and observationally testable. On the other hand, we find that current ISW and growth data remain largely in agreement. Looking ahead to Stage IV surveys we forecast improvements in constraints on the dark energy behaviour; although there will be some tightening of bounds, we argue that the problem of underdetermination will persist. We conclude that while single scalar field dark energy remains a natural and flexible framework, its ultimate viability will hinge on improved low-redshift growth measurements and a clearer understanding of gravitational screening.

### [57] [Intensity fluctuations of radio halo in galaxy cluster: Insights from power spectrum estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07814)

Method: 基于610 MHz射电观测数据，提取MACSJ0014.3-302和MACSJ0152.5-2852中心射电晕区域的角功率谱（C_l），结合含幂律涨落与指数径向轮廓的模拟 halo 模型进行拟合，并与MHD湍流理论模型比较。

Conclusion: 角功率谱是研究星系团射电晕的有效新工具，适用于未来SKA等大样本巡天，有助于识别巨射电晕及探测超出光学/ X射线可见范围的微弱团内介质辐射。

Abstract: Non-thermal synchrotron emissions from radio halo allow us to study mechanisms of particle (re)acceleration, magnetic field distribution, merger history, and turbulence in the intra-cluster medium. We propose power spectrum estimation as a novel and complementary method to study galaxy clusters. We use 610 MHz observations of MACSJ0014.3-302 and MACSJ0152.5-2852 to estimate the angular power spectrum (C_l) from the central halo regions. The C_l shows excess emission only for MACSJ0014.3-302. Using simulations, we find that a halo model with power-law fluctuations, in addition to the smooth exponential radial profile, is required to explain the observed C_l. We compare the observed power-law with existing models of MHD turbulence. The method may be useful for large data from SKA, finding megahalos in other sources, or detecting faint cluster emissions beyond the visible extent.

### [58] [Multipolar structure of the local expansion rate from incomplete sky data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07821)
*João G. Vicente,Thiago S. Pereira,Ricardo G. Rodrigues,Sandro D. P. Vitenti,Vitoria M. Gomes*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用Cosmicflows-4数据，首次用对称无迹张量基重构了局部哈勃膨胀率的低阶多极矩（ℓ=1,2,3），发现偶极幅值在3.3σ水平偏离ΛCDM预期，指向(l,b)=(290°,−4°)，支持大尺度流；而四极与八极与ΛCDM一致；多极方向间无统计显著对齐。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验ΛCDM模型下局部哈勃膨胀率各向异性是否仅由小尺度速度扰动引起，特别是验证是否存在超出标准模型预测的大尺度‘整体流’（bulk flow）信号。

Method: 基于Cosmicflows-4星系距离与速度数据，在CMB静止系z∈[0.01,0.05]范围内，采用对称无迹张量基展开局部哈勃率；引入像素掩模处理天空覆盖不均问题；通过伪逆法和最大似然法两种独立方法重建全天膨胀率场，并用模拟验证鲁棒性。

Result: 偶极振幅显著偏离ΛCDM预测（3.3σ），方向为(l,b)=(290°,−4°)±5°，主要来自z∈[0.03,0.05]样本；四极与八极振幅与ΛCDM线性+弱非线性预言一致；多极极大值位置近似重合，但完整矢量结构分析未发现统计显著对齐。

Conclusion: 观测支持存在真实的大尺度偶极流信号，挑战纯ΛCDM框架下的局部动力学解释；而更高阶多极与标准模型兼容，表明该异常可能源于特定尺度或物理机制，需进一步理论建模与数据验证。

Abstract: Using the Cosmicflows-4 data, we reconstruct the first multipolar moments of a general function describing the local expansion rate. In addition to the conventional harmonic approach, we employ a basis of symmetric and trace-free tensors to characterize the anisotropies of the expansion rate, allowing us to identify all directions associated with each of its multipoles. Focusing on objects in $z\in[0.01,0.05]$ in the CMB rest frame, we derive all $2\ell+1$ degrees of freedom in the multipoles $\ell=1,2$ and 3, which are split into one amplitude and $\ell$ unit vectors per multipole. To mitigate anisotropies induced by incomplete sky coverage, we introduce a pixel-based mask that removes poorly sampled pixels. The full-sky expansion rate is reconstructed using two independent approaches: a pseudo-inverse of the multipole-coupling kernel induced by the mask, and a maximum-likelihood estimate of the underlying full-sky field. These approaches are validated through simulations that explore different mask resolutions, cosmic variance and statistical noise. We find that the quadrupole and octupole amplitudes are consistent (at $95\%$ C.L.) with the expectations of a $Λ$CDM universe with linear and mild nonlinear perturbations, where the anisotropies of the expansion rate result from small peculiar velocities. The dipole amplitude, however, is inconsistent with $Λ$CDM predictions at 3.3$σ$, with a direction $(l, b) = (290^\circ, -4^\circ) \pm 5^\circ$ consistent with a bulk flow. This signal comes predominantly from sources in $z\in[0.03,0.05]$. Finally, we conduct alignment tests between the dipole, quadrupole, and octupole vectors. We confirm recent findings showing that the maxima of these multipoles are approximately located at $(290^\circ,-4^\circ)$. However, detailed tests using the complete vector structure of these multipoles reveal no evidence of alignments.

  <summary>Details</summary>
